# Algorithm Catalog

This section lists QTT algorithms/tools as implemented in the monorepo (by file + exported symbols).


## archive (6)

- **_archived_dense/tci_als.py**
  - `function tci_als` (L24) ‚Äî Build QTT via TCI with Alternating Least Squares refinement.
- **_archived_dense/tci_greedy.py**
  - `function tci_greedy` (L17) ‚Äî Build QTT via greedy TCI (TT-cross approximation).
  - `function tci_als_simple` (L162) ‚Äî ALS-style TCI: Initialize randomly, then optimize via alternating least squares.
  - `function _build_left_env` (L267) ‚Äî Build left environment for site k: product of cores[0:k] at given indices.
  - `function _build_right_env` (L291) ‚Äî Build right environment for site k: product of cores[k+1:] at given indices.
  - `function _evaluate_qtt_batch` (L314) ‚Äî Evaluate QTT at batch of indices.
- **_archived_dense/tci_production.py**
  - `function maxvol_pivots` (L37) ‚Äî MaxVol algorithm: find r rows of (n√ór) matrix A that maximize determinant.
  - `function tci_production` (L86) ‚Äî Production-grade TCI with PROPER skeleton decomposition.
  - `function validate_tci` (L338) ‚Äî Validate TCI reconstruction against true function values.
- **_archived_dense/tci_v2.py**
  - `function tci_correct` (L21) ‚Äî Build QTT using correct TCI with SVD-based construction.
  - `function tci_with_sweeps` (L167) ‚Äî TCI with forward-backward sweeps for refinement.
  - `function _evaluate_qtt_at_indices` (L290) ‚Äî Evaluate QTT at given indices.
- **archive/rns_qtt_ntt_butterfly_mpo_deprecated.py**
  - `class RNSPrime` (L51) ‚Äî NTT-friendly prime for RNS decomposition.
  - `function find_primitive_root` (L61) ‚Äî Find smallest primitive root modulo p.
  - `class RNSContext` (L134) ‚Äî Context for RNS arithmetic operations.
  - `function get_rns_context` (L280) ‚Äî Get default RNS context for Baby Bear field.
  - `class QTTState` (L292) ‚Äî Quantized Tensor Train representation of a vector.
  - `function build_butterfly_mpo` (L542) ‚Äî Build butterfly MPO for stage k of NTT.
  - `function apply_mpo_to_qtt` (L623) ‚Äî Apply MPO to QTT state: |œà'‚ü© = MPO |œà‚ü©
  - `function apply_butterfly_stage` (L671) ‚Äî Apply one butterfly stage to QTT state.
  - `class RNSQTTNTT` (L697) ‚Äî RNS-QTT-NTT: High-performance NTT using Residue Number System + QTT.
  - `function validate_rns_qtt_ntt` (L1046) ‚Äî Validate RNS-QTT-NTT against reference implementation.
  - `function benchmark_compression` (L1083) ‚Äî Benchmark QTT compression on different input types.

  - `function benchmark_hybrid` (L69) ‚Äî Benchmark hybrid: decompress ‚Üí flux ‚Üí recompress.
  - `function benchmark_tci` (L126) ‚Äî Benchmark TCI flux construction.
  - `function main` (L169)

  - `function small_grid_size` (L9) ‚Äî Small grid size for quick benchmark tests.
  - `function medium_grid_size` (L15) ‚Äî Medium grid size for moderate benchmark tests.
